Fabrics




Our Acrylic fabrics – Fabrics made from 100 % solution-dyed acrylic fibre, are designed especially for the preparation of awnings. The acrylic fabrics offer high levels of UV protection, Ultraviolet Protection Factor (UPF) of up to +80 according to international standard UV Standard 801.

The fabric goes through finishing Process that offers exceptional repellency to water and dirt, superior dimensional stability, and creates a durable fabric that keeps its aesthetic allure over the lifetime.

We offer upto 10 Years Warranty on selected Fabrics*

Awnings Styles


India Awnings helps you create an ambience to your outdoors, whether you need an Awnings to shade your balconies and windows, enjoy your patio, beautify your terrace, or to get a shade for your car parking, we have you covered.



Retractable Awnings also Known as Balcony Awnings / Terrace Awnings / Patio Awning

Whether you need an Awnings to simply enjoy your patio, or to attract customers to your retail space, we have a solution. Our high quality Awnings products have a very functional European look that when extended slopes down in a straight line and is engineered for durability and quality.

All of our awnings are constructed with high quality exterior grade pure polyester powder coated frames.
We offer 10 year Warranty* on exclusive range of European fabrics

Retractable awning: The  retractable patio Awnings is easy to operate and is virtually maintenance free and self storing when not in use.This Premium Quality product is suitable with almost any kind of Outdoor Fabric .All our Retractable awnings are custom manufactured to provide a fully retractable product that is easy to operate, maintenance free . This makes outdoor living inviting and safe from the sun’s harmful UV rays.




Free Standing Retractable Awnings also known as Garden Awning: The Garden Awning is a free standing retractable Awnings system. it provides protection from the sun’s harmful rays and light rain, virtually anywhere you desire. When not in use, the Awnings can be fully retracted making it worry free. If you ever considered a retractable Awnings but had no place to mount it on your structure, then the Garden Awnings free standing Awnings is your answer.




Retractable Awnings with Drop Valance: The Awnings with Drop Valance is is available on both the  Wall mounted awnings as well as Free standing retractable awning. When retracted the adjustable valance is Rolled up and if so chosen , tucked neatly behind the standard front valance. These specially designed fabrics allow visibility out while permitting filtered light to enter without the annoying glare.




(Parts may Vary depending on the model , please contact sales representative to learn about key components in detail)

Door , Window & Canopy Awnings

Adding the right custom-made canopy to your building can instantly transform it into a showstopper. Canopy awnings cast full shade on your windows while still retaining the view, making them extremely effective for heat control, as they stop sun rays from reaching the interior of your home.  At India Awning. We will make your canopy individually, and tailor it to your exact style, shape, and size specifications.

All of our awnings are constructed with high quality exterior grade pure polyester powder coated frames.
We offer 10 year Warranty* on exclusive range of European fabrics

Basket Awnings : The Basket Awnings series canopy awnings can be ordered in a variety of widths, heights, and projections  Operation can be pull cord or fixed frames for stationery units. Multiple colours are available, either solution-dyed acrylic Awnings fabric or vinyl Awnings fabric, that are long lasting and completely colour fast





Duchess Awning:The Duchess Awnings is a Canopy Awnings made from Custom bent single piece of Extruded aluminium. Can be operating or fixed.Graphics can be applied to valance or body between bows . Multiple colours are available, either solution-dyed acrylic Awnings fabric or vinyl Awnings fabric, that are long lasting and completely colour fast.





Drop Arm Awnings : All of our Drop arm awnings are fully adjustable and retractable, the Awnings can drop down to desired length & fully cover a window if so desired, and virtually disappear against the face of the building when not in use - providing complete control over the amount of sunlight that enters a room.





Diplomat Awning: The Diplomat Awnings series canopy awnings can be ordered in a variety of width, height and projections.also referred to as quarterball awnings. Multiple colours are available, either solution-dyed acrylic Awnings fabric or vinyl Awnings fabric, that are long lasting and completely colour fast.




Visage Awning: The Visage Awnings series canopy awnings can be ordered in a variety of width, height and projections. . Multiple colours are available, either solution-dyed acrylic Awnings fabric or vinyl Awnings fabric, that are long lasting and completely colour fast.





Traditional awning: The Traditional Awnings series canopy awnings can be ordered in a variety of width, height and projections. . Multiple colours are available, either solution-dyed acrylic Awnings fabric or vinyl Awnings fabric, that are long lasting and completely colour fast.





(Parts may Vary depending on the model , please contact sales representative to learn about key components in detail)



Vertical Awnings/ Drop Awnings

Our vertical awnings are a functional and unobtrusive sun shading system for vertical facades and large window areas. They offer the necessary protection against sunlight to keep room temperatures at a pleasantly cool level. For this reason, vertical awnings are effective both on private homes and on commercial buildings. . Multiple colours are available, either solution-dyed acrylic Awnings fabric or vinyl Awnings fabric, that are long lasting and completely colour fast.

Thanks to their small installation dimensions, vertical awnings are particularly well suited for retrofitting on windows where space is limited.

All of our awnings are constructed with high quality exterior grade pure polyester powder coated frames.
We offer 10 year Warranty* on exclusive range of European fabrics

(Parts may Vary depending on the model , please contact sales representative to learn about key components in detail)

Tensile membranes structures & Shade sail Structures

Our experience & Design capabilities combined with in house Steel structure fabrication unit enables us to design, fabricate and erect the most suitable Tensile membrane structures for your needs Tensile membrane structures can be used for various application like roof top restaurents, private terrace and gardens , tensile membrane car parking structures ,Tensile membrane shade sail for courtyards verandah’s and in open passages for sunshade protection. As a high degree of customization is required we request you to consult our technical team for furtherance in this regard.

All of our awnings are constructed with high quality exterior grade pure polyester powder coated frames.
We offer 10 year Warranty* on exclusive range of European fabrics
